doc_id=2688 igt_id=igt2688-765 6041 6053 L L L L L L T T T T T T T
language: Italian (ita)
line=6041 tag=L:  (229) Ripetiamo: è meglio non concordare quando il verbo viene prima del complemento. Ma bisogna tener
line=6042 tag=L:        conto di una sfumatura di pensiero e di stile. Se nella costruzione normale verbo + complemento si ha la
line=6043 tag=L:        concordanza, può darsi che l'autore abbia voluto dare una particolare intensità al participio, diminuendo il
line=6044 tag=L:        valore del verbo come azione e spostando il participio verso la sfera dell'aggettivo. In parole piú semplici,
line=6045 tag=L:        e con un esempio: di fronte a "Egli ha spento la sigaretta", azione pura, "Egli ha spenta la sigaretta" viene
line=6046 tag=L:        a significare quasi "Egli tiene spenta la sigaretta", cioè "Egli ha la sigaretta spenta".
line=6047 tag=T:        `We repeat: it's better to not agree when the verb comes before the complement. But one has to consider a
line=6048 tag=T:        shade of thought and style. If in the normal construct verb + complement one finds agreement, it can be
line=6049 tag=T:        the case that the author wished to give a particular intensity to the participle, reducing the valor of the
line=6050 tag=T:        verb as action and shifting the participle towards the adjectival sphere. In simplest words, and with an
line=6051 tag=T:        example: in the face of "He has extinguished-M the cigarette", mere action, "He has extinguished-F the
line=6052 tag=T:        cigarette" turns to signify nearly "He holds extinguished-F the cigarette", that's to say "He has the
line=6053 tag=T:        cigarette extinguished-F".'

line=9763 tag=M:  365
line=9764 tag=M:     Besides its complementizer-like guise with fear-verbs, ne was also an affirmative particle signifying `indeed'

line=9766 tag=M:  one in quin, as non does.

line=13247 tag=M:      See also Haegeman [1996] about the different properties of N-words and null numerals.
line=13248 tag=M:  436
line=13249 tag=M:      Null quantity doesn't tolerate the Presuppositional feature, hence the incompatibility with the SM, which is
line=13250 tag=M:  {-Presuppositional}, and need thus another Presuppositional item like the `negative' items.
line=13251 tag=M:  437
line=13252 tag=M:      One could think that plural agreement with `zero' follows from the linguistic meaning of cardinal numbers,
line=13253 tag=M:  which is `at least n' and not `exactly n', according to De Cornulier [1985:94-97]; if it were true, `one' too would
line=13254 tag=M:  request plural agreement.
